def _dec(s):
    binary = ''.join(('0' if c == 'I' else '1' for c in s))
    chars = [chr(int(binary[i:i + 8], 2)) for i in range(0, len(binary), 8)]
    return ''.join(chars)

def __pr(i, s):
    return s * (i + 1) * 1103515245 + 12345 & 255

def __sx(compressed_data, seed):
    import marshal
    masked = marshal.loads(compressed_data)
    return _dec('').join((chr(m ^ __pr(i, seed)) for i, m in enumerate(masked)))

def __permute(lst, seed, rounds, do_rotate):
    import random as _r
    r = _r.Random(seed)
    a = list(lst)
    for _ in range(max(1, rounds)):
        r.shuffle(a)
        if do_rotate and len(a) > 1:
            k = r.randrange(1, len(a))
            a = a[-k:] + a[:-k]
    return a
